I’m tired of feeling behind before the day’s even started, so I’m focusing on doing a few things better instead of trying to do everything.

Here’s what’s helping me reset:

• I’m getting clear on what I actually want from 2026, not just vague goals
• I’m keeping my daily routine simple so it’s easier to stick to
• I’m checking in with my mood and energy, not just my to-do list
• I’m noticing small wins instead of brushing past them
• I’m making space for self-care and reflection, even if it’s just a few minutes
